posted:Posted October 5, 2023
msg:Environment: The hotel is old, and it can be seen in the lobby. Ctrip shows that some room types were renovated in 2018, mainly the executive floors (14th/15th floor). The renovated room is quite nice.

Service: After communication, the manager upgraded to the executive floor, and the experience is much better. However, when room availability permits, the front desk does not take the initiative to upgrade rooms to improve guest experience like the current average star hotels.
